Trigger V0010_Standard_Battle_Attacker_Crushing_Victory_VnV_Trigger
    WhenToTest PostBattle

    Condition WasAttacker
          and IsGeneral
          and WonBattle
          and BattleSuccess = crushing
          and I_ConflictType Normal
          and not BattleOdds < 0.35
          and BattleOdds < 1.2
          and PercentageEnemyKilled > 25
          and not Trait Bug = 1

    Affects GoodAttacker  4  Chance  100 
    Affects TacticalSkill  2  Chance  10 

;Mod507 - 02/28 : changed battleodds
;Mod335 - 02/14 : increased tacticalskill chance to 10 from 5
;Mod185 - 11/03 : reduced battle odds to 0.25

;Section12c - Mission Completed
;===============================================================
;------------------------------------------
Trigger senate5
    WhenToTest LeaderSenateMissionSuccess


    Affects PlainRomanVirtue  1  Chance  10 

;------------------------------------------
;===============================================================
;Section13 - Triggers For New Traits
;===============================================================

;------------------------------------------
Trigger 1fastagent
   WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

   Condition Trait FastAgent < 1

   Affects FastAgent  1  Chance  100 

;------------------------------------------
Trigger 2fastagent
   WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

   Condition Trait FastAgent2 < 1

   Affects FastAgent2  1  Chance  100 

;------------------------------------------
Trigger 3fastagent
   WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

   Condition Trait FastAgent3 < 1

   Affects FastAgent3  1  Chance  100 

;Mod516 - 02/28 : new trigger, adding to double trigger bugfix
;------------------------------------------
Trigger general_lame
   WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

   Condition Trait BattleScarred > 4

   Affects Lame  1  Chance  5 

;GAFHMod7 - 4/1 : new trigger to acquire new trait
;------------------------------------------
;===============================================================
;Section14 - Academy Triggers
;===============================================================
;------------------------------------------
;------------------------------------------
Trigger academy
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition EndedInSettlement
          and RemainingMPPercentage = 100
          and SettlementBuildingExists >= academy

    Affects MathematicsSkill  2  Chance  1 
    Affects RhetoricSkill  2  Chance  1 
    Affects SmoothTalker  2  Chance  1 
    Affects PoeticSkill  2  Chance  1 
    Affects PhilosophySkill  2  Chance  1 
    Affects Aesthetic  2  Chance  1 

;------------------------------------------
Trigger scriptorium
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition EndedInSettlement
          and RemainingMPPercentage = 100
          and SettlementBuildingExists >= scriptorium

    Affects NaturalPhilosophySkill  2  Chance  1 
    Affects ArchitectSkill  2  Chance  1 
    Affects GoodEngineer  2  Chance  1 
    Affects GoodAdministrator  2  Chance  1 
    Affects PublicAtheism  2  Chance  1 

;------------------------------------------
Trigger ludus_magnus
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition EndedInSettlement
          and RemainingMPPercentage = 100
          and SettlementBuildingExists = ludus_magnus

    Affects StrategicSkill  2  Chance  1 
    Affects LogisticalSkill  2  Chance  1 
    Affects TacticalSkill  4  Chance  1 
    Affects PoliticsSkill  6  Chance  1 
    Affects Pragmatic  2  Chance  1 

;Mod460 - 02/25 : doubled tacticalskill effect
;------------------------------------------
Trigger recurring1
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition EndedInSettlement
          and RemainingMPPercentage = 100
          and SettlementBuildingExists >= academy
          and Trait MathematicsSkill > 0

    Affects MathematicsSkill  1  Chance  10 
    Affects NaturalPhilosophySkill  1  Chance  5 
    Affects GoodEngineer  1  Chance  5 

;------------------------------------------
Trigger recurring2
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition EndedInSettlement
          and RemainingMPPercentage = 100
          and SettlementBuildingExists >= academy
          and Trait RhetoricSkill > 0

    Affects RhetoricSkill  1  Chance  10 

;------------------------------------------
Trigger recurring3
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition EndedInSettlement
          and RemainingMPPercentage = 100
          and SettlementBuildingExists >= academy
          and Trait SmoothTalker > 0

    Affects SmoothTalker  1  Chance  10 

;------------------------------------------
Trigger recurring4
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition EndedInSettlement
          and RemainingMPPercentage = 100
          and SettlementBuildingExists >= academy
          and Trait PoeticSkill > 0

    Affects PoeticSkill  1  Chance  10 

;------------------------------------------

;------------------------------------------
;------------------------------------------
Trigger games
    WhenToTest GovernorThrowGames


    Affects GamesFanRomanVice  1  Chance  10 

;------------------------------------------
Trigger races
    WhenToTest GovernorThrowRaces


    Affects RacesFanRomanVice  1  Chance  10 

;------------------------------------------
Trigger assassininit4
    WhenToTest AgentCreated

    Condition AgentType = assassin
          and SettlementBuildingExists = great_forum

    Affects GoodAssassin  1  Chance  100 

;Mod291 - 02/10 : changed effect to goodassassin from natural assassin skill
;------------------------------------------
Trigger assassininit5
    WhenToTest AgentCreated

    Condition AgentType = assassin
          and SettlementBuildingExists = curia

    Affects GoodAssassin  2  Chance  100 

;Mod292 - 02/10 : changed effect to goodassassin from natural assassin skill
;------------------------------------------
Trigger spying_target
    WhenToTest ExecutesASpyOnAMission


    Affects CounterSpy  1  Chance  100 

;------------------------------------------
Trigger assassination_target
    WhenToTest ExecutesAnAssassinOnAMission


    Affects AssassinCatcher  1  Chance  100 


;------------------------------------------
;===============================================================
;Section16 - Age-Related Triggers
;===============================================================
;------------------------------------------
;------------------------------------------
Trigger general_ages_one_turn
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition AgentType = family
	    and Trait CharacterAges = 1

    Affects TurnsAlive  1  Chance  100    
    

;GAFHMod34 - 4/4 : trait increments each season, adjust thresholds accordingly if more than 2 seasons/year
;------------------------------------------
Trigger diplomat_ages_one_turn
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition not IsGeneral   	
          and AgentType = diplomat         
          and Trait CharacterAges = 1

    Affects DiplomatTurnsAlive  1  Chance  100    
    

;GAFHMod45 - 4/5 : trait increments each season, adjust thresholds accordingly if more than 2 seasons/year
;------------------------------------------
Trigger spy_ages_one_turn
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition not IsGeneral   	
          and AgentType = spy         
          and Trait CharacterAges = 1

    Affects SpyTurnsAlive  1  Chance  100    
    

;GAFHMod40 - 4/4 : trait increments each season, adjust thresholds accordingly if more than 2 seasons/year
;------------------------------------------
Trigger assassin_ages_one_turn
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition not IsGeneral	       	
          and AgentType = assassin	   
	    and Trait CharacterAges = 1

    Affects AssassinTurnsAlive  1  Chance  100    
    

;GAFHMod44 - 4/4 : trait increments each season, adjust thresholds accordingly if more than 2 seasons/year
;------------------------------------------
Trigger general_starting_age
    WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

    Affects TurnsAlive  1  Chance  100
    Affects CharacterAges  1  Chance  100
    

;GAFHMod35 - 4/4 : starting age of general

;;ROP2.2 - political triggers

;;Character comes of age
;Faction Leader's political orientation
;------------------------------------------
Trigger birth_politics_follow_my_leader_dem
    WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

    Condition FactionLeaderTrait Democracy >= 1

    Affects Democracy  1  Chance  70 

;------------------------------------------
Trigger birth_politics_follow_my_leader_oli
    WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

    Condition FactionLeaderTrait Oligarchy >= 1

    Affects Oligarchy  1  Chance  70 

;------------------------------------------
Trigger birth_politics_follow_my_leader_mon
    WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

    Condition FactionLeaderTrait Monarchy >= 1

    Affects Monarchy  1  Chance  70 

;Athens-specific
;------------------------------------------
Trigger birth_politics_athens_dem_1
    WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

    Condition FactionType seleucid
    			and I_TurnNumber < 80
          and Trait Monarchy = 0
          and Trait Oligarchy = 0
          and Trait Democracy = 0

    Affects Democracy  1  Chance  30

          and EndedInSettlement
          and RemainingMPPercentage = 100
          and SettlementBuildingExists >= gov_monarchy2

    Affects MonarchyConversion  1  Chance  3 
    Affects MonarchyConversion_Greek  1  Chance  3
